namespace = startup

########################################################################################
# startup
########################################################################################
country_event = {
	id = startup.1
	title = "startup.1.t"
	desc = "startup.1.d"
	picture = culture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = game_start_flag }
		ai = no
	}
	
	immediate = {
		#One time only scripted effects
		iu_initialize_schools_effect = yes
		initialize_chinese_schools_effect = yes
		initialize_polis_modifiers = yes
		set_wonder_flags_start_effect = yes
		upgrade_great_project_history_effect = yes
		sub_roman_core_cleanup_effect = yes
		#################################
		set_global_flag = game_start_flag
		# Popgrowth
		set_global_flag = popgrowth_vanilla	
		set_global_flag = coloredvassals_ai_yes
		country_event = { id = startup.2 }	# adds popgrowth base values
		
		every_country = {
			# Institutions
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_institution = writing_system } }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = illiterate_country_modifier
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_institution = iron_age } }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = bronze_age_modifier
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			
			# Estates
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_estate = estate_priesthood
					has_estate = estate_merchants
					has_estate = estate_nobility
				}
				change_estate_land_share = {
					estate = estate_priesthood
					share = -6
				}
				change_estate_land_share = {
					estate = estate_merchants
					share = -3
				}
				change_estate_land_share = {
					estate = estate_nobility
					share = 22
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_estate = estate_clans }
				change_estate_land_share = {
					estate = estate_clans
					share = 20
				}
			}
		}
		
		# Slavery
		
		every_country = {
			export_to_variable = { which = slaves value = total_development }
			# effect of total development: 30% to 10% total value
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = total_development
				1000 = { multiply_variable = { slaves = 1.01 } } # 10%
				500 = { multiply_variable = { slaves = 1.2 } }	
				200 = { multiply_variable = { slaves = 1.5 } }	# 15%: 250 dev = 2.500.000 population x 15% = 375.000. 250 x 1.5 = 375 (thousand). OK
				100 = { multiply_variable = { slaves = 1.8 } }	
				50 = { multiply_variable = { slaves = 2.5 }	}
				10 = { multiply_variable = { slaves = 3.0 }	}
				1 = { multiply_variable = { slaves = 3.5 } }	# 4 dev = 40.000 population x 35% = 14000. 4 x 3.5 = 14. OK
			}
			set_country_flag = SD_priv_recent_change		# updater for privileges
			
			# Assign slave types by government type. Values: Native -60%, Tribal -30%, Republics -10%, Oligarchy 0%, Monarchy +10%
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = government
				native = { 			# shouldn't have slaves estate, anyway
					multiply_variable = { slaves = 0.4 } 
					set_estate_privilege = estate_slaves_status_1 	# war captives
					set_estate_privilege = estate_slaves_jobs_1		# farming and mining
				}	
				tribal = { 			# shouldn't have slaves estate, anyway
					multiply_variable = { slaves = 0.7 } 
					set_estate_privilege = estate_slaves_status_1 	# war captives
					set_estate_privilege = estate_slaves_jobs_1		# farming and mining
				}
				republic = { 
					multiply_variable = { slaves = 0.9 } 
					set_estate_privilege = estate_slaves_status_3 	# normal type
					set_estate_privilege = estate_slaves_jobs_2		# normal use
				}
				theocracy = { 	# oligarchy
					set_estate_privilege = estate_slaves_status_3 	# normal type
					set_estate_privilege = estate_slaves_jobs_1		# farming and mining
				}
				monarchy = { 
					multiply_variable = { slaves = 1.10 } 
					set_estate_privilege = estate_slaves_status_2 	# serfdom
					set_estate_privilege = estate_slaves_jobs_1		# farming and mining
				}
				
			}
			set_estate_privilege = estate_slaves_condition_3		# 3 is normal. Ranges from 1 to 7
			change_estate_land_share = { estate = estate_slaves share = -100 }
			
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = { SD_slavesprod_check = yes }
				SD_update_provslots = yes
			}
		}
		
		# Flag, to remove naval forcelimit from inland provinces, and -50% in "river ports"
		PG_add_river_ports = yes
		
		# Correct production buildings where they are not correct
		every_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = { has_building = small_water_irrigation has_building = big_water_irrigation has_building = big_estate }
				NOT = { trade_goods = grain } 	NOT = { trade_goods = wine }	NOT = { trade_goods = spices }
				NOT = { trade_goods = fruits }	NOT = { trade_goods = olive  }	NOT = { trade_goods = rice }
				NOT = { trade_goods = tea_good } NOT = { trade_goods = horses }	NOT = { trade_goods = honey }
				NOT = { trade_goods = olibanum } NOT = { trade_goods = herbs  } NOT = { trade_goods = cotton  }
				NOT = { trade_goods = opium } NOT = { trade_goods = sugar }
			}
			correct_production_tradegood = yes
		}
		every_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = { has_building = craftsman  has_building = small_workshop  has_building = artisan_district  }
				NOT = { trade_goods = wool }	NOT = { trade_goods = cloth }	NOT = { trade_goods = fish }
				NOT = { trade_goods = fur }		NOT = { trade_goods = naval_supplies }	NOT = { trade_goods = amber }
				NOT = { trade_goods = paper }	NOT = { trade_goods = ceramic }	NOT = { trade_goods = meat_animals }
				NOT = { trade_goods = dyes }	NOT = { trade_goods = silk }
				NOT = { trade_goods = glas }	NOT = { trade_goods = pearls }   NOT = { trade_goods = exotic_animals  }
				NOT = { trade_goods = ivory }	NOT = { trade_goods = tar_good } NOT = { trade_goods = metalware }
				
			}
			correct_production_tradegood = yes
		}
		every_province = {
			limit = {
				OR = { has_building = quarry has_building = small_mine has_building = big_mine }
				NOT = { trade_goods = salt } 	NOT = { trade_goods = copper }	NOT = { trade_goods = iron }
				NOT = { trade_goods = marble }	NOT = { trade_goods = lead }	NOT = { trade_goods = tin }
				NOT = { trade_goods = gems  }	NOT = { trade_goods = silver }	NOT = { trade_goods = gold }
				NOT = { trade_goods = jade  }
			}
			correct_production_tradegood = yes
		}
		
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				government = monarchy
				has_consort_regency = no
				has_regency = no
			}
			add_ruler_modifier = { name = coronation_decent }
			set_ruler_flag = ruler_coronation
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "startup.1.a"	
		
	}
}

########################################################################################
# startup - POPULATION GROWTH, or, why is there a limit into my province's population. By Mrkcosta (discord, @mrkcosta.9274)
########################################################################################
country_event = {
	id = startup.2
	title = "startup.2.t"
	desc = "startup.2.d"
	picture = celebration_priestess
	major = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes		# Fired by the popgrowth menu, in the country decisions
	
	#trigger = {
	#	NOT = { has_global_flag = popgrowth_initiated }
	#	NOT = { ai = yes }
	#}
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = popgrowth_initiated	# always
		clr_global_flag = popgrowth_vanilla		# disables the vanilla growth mechanism
		set_global_flag = popgrowth_running		# applies the mod itself, all other events
		
		
		
		# here comes the BIG part of the population mod. Basically this gives each province a "province size" that is used to define how much population it can sustain. Then this will be multiplied by any variable that affects agriculture (ie winters, monsoons, aridity); some of those can be offset with technology or certain buildings. 
		# anyway, this number is the base tribal number, so if a province has got value 5, it may sustain 5 tribal pops. More capacity than current population, will allow it to keep growing. 
		# to get this number, I have exported the provinces.bmp map into a third-party program that is able to export each RGB color (every province, in the definitions of a PDX game) into pixel count, thus showing the province size in pixels of each province. After discarding PTI, water, mountains, etc; this is the 1-to-10 scale:
		# 1: 1 to 50 px (only islands and such)
		# 2: 50 to 150 px (delta 100)
		# 3: 150 to 275 px (delta 125)
		# 4: 275 to 425 px (delta 150)
		# 5: 425 to 600 px (delta 175)
		# 6: 600 to 825 px (delta 225)
		# 7: 825 to 1.100 px (delta 275)
		# 8: 1.100 to 1.425 px (delta 325)
		# 9: 1.425 to 1.800 px (delta 375)
		# 10: over 1.800 px. Actually goes up to 20, but in very few cases. The last count is 539 provs (out of 7.976 active ones, 7%)
		
		hidden_effect = {
			
			# Remember to keep updating this database. Last update: 02/04/2023 (Popgrowth version 4, sizes up to 20)
			
			1 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 4 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 1 } } # Bonus of 1
			2 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 3 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 2 } } # Bonus of 1
			3 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 3 } }
			4 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 4 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 4 } } # Bonus of 1
			5 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 4 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 5 } } # Bonus of 1
			6 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 6 } }
			7 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 4 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 7 } } # Bonus of 1
			8 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 3 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 8 } } # Bonus of 1
			9 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 4 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 9 } } # Bonus of 1
			10 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 3 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 10 } } # Bonus of 1
			11 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 3 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 11 } } # Bonus of 1
			12 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 4 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 12 } } # Bonus of 1
			13 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 1 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 13 } }
			14 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 14 } }
			15 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 3 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 15 } } # Bonus of 1
			16 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 16 } }
			17 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 3 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 17 } } # Bonus of 1
			18 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 3 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 18 } }
			19 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 19 } }
			20 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 3 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 20 } }
			21 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 21 } }
			22 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 3 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 22 } }

			119 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 6 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 119 } } # Bonus of 1
			120 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 3 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 120 } } # Bonus of 1
			121 = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 2 } set_variable = { which = prov_id_base value = 121 } }

			# Final: assign modifier into the world map (visible through the Trade Mapmode, and paused) and other things
			
			every_province = {
				# Show the province size in the trade mapmode; for the first days only
				if = { 		limit = { check_variable = { prov_size = 11 } } add_province_modifier = { name = PS_provsize11 duration = 30 } }
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { prov_size = 10 } } add_province_modifier = { name = PS_provsize10 duration = 30 } }
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { prov_size = 9 } }  add_province_modifier = { name = PS_provsize09 duration = 30 } }
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { prov_size = 8 } }  add_province_modifier = { name = PS_provsize08 duration = 30 } }
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { prov_size = 7 } }  add_province_modifier = { name = PS_provsize07 duration = 30 } }
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { prov_size = 6 } }  add_province_modifier = { name = PS_provsize06 duration = 30 } }
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { prov_size = 5 } }  add_province_modifier = { name = PS_provsize05 duration = 30 } }
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { prov_size = 4 } }  add_province_modifier = { name = PS_provsize04 duration = 30 } }
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { prov_size = 3 } }  add_province_modifier = { name = PS_provsize03 duration = 30 } }
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { prov_size = 2 } }  add_province_modifier = { name = PS_provsize02 duration = 30 } }
				else_if = { limit = { check_variable = { prov_size = 1 } }  add_province_modifier = { name = PS_provsize01 duration = 30 } }
				else = { set_variable = { which = prov_size value = 1 } 	add_province_modifier = { name = PS_provsize_no duration = 30 } }
				
				export_to_variable = { which = PS_trb_init value = base_manpower }
				export_to_variable = { which = PS_urb_init value = base_production }
				export_to_variable = { which = PS_upp_init value = base_tax }
				export_to_variable = { which = PS_tot_init value = development }
				export_to_variable = { which = PS_year_init value = trigger_value:is_year }	# all used for statistics tracking
				
				province_event = { id = population_capacity.4 }	# new version, v4.0
				
				# adding conditions, in case that the starting dev > capacity. Gives 100-year exception to migration and demotion
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = PS_trb_init which = PG_trb_cap } }
					add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = rural_pause duration = 36500 hidden = yes }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { check_variable = { which = PS_urb_init which = PG_com_cap } }
					add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = urban_pause duration = 36500 hidden = yes }
				}
				
				# In case a province does not have the mine modifier present
				trigger_switch = {
					on_trigger = trade_goods
					gold = { 	DE_check_minimum_production_startup = { metal = gold } set_province_flag = DE_2years }
					silver = { 	DE_check_minimum_production_startup = { metal = silver } set_province_flag = DE_2years }
					copper = { 	DE_check_minimum_production_startup = { metal = copper } set_province_flag = DE_2years }
					iron = { 	DE_check_minimum_production_startup = { metal = iron } set_province_flag = DE_2years }
					lead = { 	DE_check_minimum_production_startup = { metal = lead } set_province_flag = DE_2years }
					tin = { 	DE_check_minimum_production_startup = { metal = tin } set_province_flag = DE_2years }
					marble = { 	DE_check_minimum_production_startup = { metal = marble } set_province_flag = DE_2years }
					gems = { 	DE_check_minimum_production_startup = { metal = gems } set_province_flag = DE_2years }
					jade = { 	DE_check_minimum_production_startup = { metal = jade } set_province_flag = DE_2years }
					
				}
				
				# Production and value, to find trade node capacity
				DE_update_goods = yes
				DE_update_value = yes
				
			}
			
		}
		
	}
	
	option = {
		name = "startup.2.a"	
		hidden_effect = {
			every_province = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_province_modifier = popgrowth_viewer } NOT = { has_province_modifier = popgrowth_viewer2 } }
					add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = popgrowth_viewer duration = -1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = { 
	    hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = sieges.3 } }
	}
}

#Changes estate land arrangement
country_event = {
	id = startup.7
	title = "startup.6.t"
	desc = "startup.6.d"
	picture = culture
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {}
	
	option = {
	    name = "startup.6.a"
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { has_estate = estate_clans }
				has_estate = estate_priesthood
				has_estate = estate_merchants
				has_estate = estate_nobility
			}
		}
		change_estate_land_share = {
			estate = estate_priesthood
			share = -7
		}
		change_estate_land_share = {
			estate = estate_merchants
			share = -4
		}
		change_estate_land_share = {
			estate = estate_nobility
			share = 22
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_estate = estate_clans }
			change_estate_land_share = {
				estate = estate_clans
				share = 30
			}
		}
	}
}

			add_bookmark_help_modifier = yes
		}
	}

	    name = "startup.8.a"
		add_years_of_income = 2 
	}
}
